<script>
	function clear_click() {
		var inp = document.getElementById("arFilterNAME");
		inp.value = "";
		get_filtered_items();
	}

	var jsControl = new JCTitleBox({
		'AJAX_PAGE' : '/bitrix/templates/corp_services_orange/ajax/search_items.php',
		'CONTAINER_ID': 'search__inputwr',
		'INPUT_ID': 'arFilterNAME',
		'INPUT_UID': 'arFilterNAME_ID',
		'MIN_QUERY_LEN': 3,
		'MODE': 'items'});

	function extended_filter_click(obj)
		{
			set_unset_filter(obj);
			var ext_div = document.getElementById("extended_filter_line");
			if (ext_div.style.display == 'block')
				{ext_div.style.display = 'none';}
			else
				{ext_div.style.display = 'block';}

		}
	function onArticleInput_press(e)
		{
		  if (e.which == null)
			{
				if (e.keyCode != 13)
				return null;

			}
			if (e.which != 0 && e.charCode != 0)
			{
				if (e.which != 13)
					return null; // спец. символ
			}
			get_filtered_items();
			return null;
		}

		function downloadPrice(file_format, pk)
		{
			var params		= '';
			var arFilters	= {};
			var child_data;
			var filters 	= $('#modal_window_div .filter_line .catalog-filtr__check:checked');
			for(var i=0; i<filters.length; i++)
			{
				child_data = filters[i];
				if(arFilters[child_data.name] == undefined)
					arFilters[child_data.name] = encodeURIComponent(child_data.value);
				else
					arFilters[child_data.name] = arFilters[child_data.name] + '||' + encodeURIComponent(child_data.value);

				if($(child_data).attr('data-new-property') == 'PROPERTY_NOVYY_TOVAR') {
					if(arFilters['PROPERTY_NOVYY_TOVAR'] == undefined)
						arFilters['PROPERTY_NOVYY_TOVAR'] = encodeURIComponent($(child_data).attr('data-new-value'));
					else
						arFilters['PROPERTY_NOVYY_TOVAR'] = arFilters['PROPERTY_NOVYY_TOVAR'] + '||' + encodeURIComponent($(child_data).attr('data-new-value'));
				}

			}
			for(var key in arFilters)
			{
				params = params + "&" + key + '=' + arFilters[key];
			}
			var cur_partner = $('#modal_window_div .parent_line .catalog-filtr__check:checked');
			console.log(cur_partner);
			var cur_partner_value = '';
			if(cur_partner.length > 0) {
				cur_partner_value = cur_partner[0].id;//value;
				params = params + '&parID=' + cur_partner_value.substring(6);
			}
			console.log(params);
			console.log('price_xls.php?FILE='+file_format+'&ACTION=FILTER' + params+'&PK='+pk);
			/*$('#main_block').hide();
			$('#close_line').hide();
			$('#waiting').show();*/
			window.location.href = 'price_xls.php?FILE='+file_format+'&ACTION=FILTER' + params+'&PK='+pk;
		}

		function downloadPricePhoto(pk)
		{
			var params		= '';
			var arFilters	= {};
			var child_data;
			var filters 	= $('#modal_window_div .filter_line .catalog-filtr__check:checked');
			for(var i=0; i<filters.length; i++)
			{
				child_data = filters[i];
				if(arFilters[child_data.name] == undefined)
					arFilters[child_data.name] = encodeURIComponent(child_data.value);
				else
					arFilters[child_data.name] = arFilters[child_data.name] + '||' + encodeURIComponent(child_data.value);

				if($(child_data).attr('data-new-property') == 'PROPERTY_NOVYY_TOVAR') {
					if(arFilters['PROPERTY_NOVYY_TOVAR'] == undefined)
						arFilters['PROPERTY_NOVYY_TOVAR'] = encodeURIComponent($(child_data).attr('data-new-value'));
					else
						arFilters['PROPERTY_NOVYY_TOVAR'] = arFilters['PROPERTY_NOVYY_TOVAR'] + '||' + encodeURIComponent($(child_data).attr('data-new-value'));
				}
			}
			for(var key in arFilters)
			{
				params = params + "&" + key + '=' + arFilters[key];
			}
			var cur_partner = $('#modal_window_div .parent_line .catalog-filtr__check:checked');
			var cur_partner_value = '';
			if(cur_partner.length > 0) {
				cur_partner_value = cur_partner[0].id;//value;
				params = params + '&parID=' + cur_partner_value.substring(6);
			}

			/*$('#main_block').hide();
			$('#close_line').hide();
			$('#waiting').show();*/
			window.location.href = 'price_xls_im.php?ACTION=FILTER' + params+'&PK='+pk;
		}


		function downloadSpec(file_format)
		{
			var href_str	= '';
			var params		= '';
			var arFilters	= {};
			var child_data;
			var filters 	= $('#modal_window_div .filter_line .catalog-filtr__check:checked');
			for(var i=0; i<filters.length; i++)
			{
				child_data = filters[i];
				if(child_data.name == 'PROPERTY_IZGOTOVITEL' && child_data.value == 'NOVOTECH') {
					href_str = 'novotech';
				}
				else if(child_data.name == 'PROPERTY_IZGOTOVITEL' && child_data.value == 'NOVOTECH LAMP') {
					href_str = 'novotech lamp';
				}
				else if(child_data.name == 'PROPERTY_IZGOTOVITEL' && child_data.value == 'ODEON LIGHT') {
					href_str = 'odeon light';
				}
				else if(child_data.name == 'PROPERTY_IZGOTOVITEL' && child_data.value == 'SONEX') {
					href_str = 'sonex';
				}
				else if(child_data.name == 'PROPERTY_IZGOTOVITEL' && child_data.value == 'LUMION') {
					href_str = 'lumion';
				}
				else if(child_data.name == 'PROPERTY_IZGOTOVITEL' && child_data.value == 'ODEON LIGHT EXCLUSIVE') {
					href_str = 'odeon light_exclusive';
				}
				else if(child_data.name == 'ALL_NEW' && child_data.value == 'ALL_NEW') {
					href_str = 'all_new';
				} else if(child_data.name == 'ALL' && child_data.value == 'ALL') {
					href_str = 'all';
				} else {
					if(arFilters[child_data.name] == undefined)
						arFilters[child_data.name] = encodeURIComponent(child_data.value);
					else
						arFilters[child_data.name] = arFilters[child_data.name] + '||' + encodeURIComponent(child_data.value);

					if($(child_data).attr('data-new-property') == 'PROPERTY_NOVYY_TOVAR')
						if(arFilters['PROPERTY_NOVYY_TOVAR'] == undefined)
							arFilters['PROPERTY_NOVYY_TOVAR'] = encodeURIComponent($(child_data).attr('data-new-value'));
						else
							arFilters['PROPERTY_NOVYY_TOVAR'] = arFilters['PROPERTY_NOVYY_TOVAR'] + '||' + encodeURIComponent($(child_data).attr('data-new-value'));
				}

				if($(child_data).attr('data-new-property') == 'PROPERTY_NOVYY_TOVAR' && href_str != '') {
					href_str = href_str + '_new';
				}
			}
			for(var key in arFilters)
			{
				params = params + "&" + key + '=' + arFilters[key];
			}
			var cur_partner = $('#modal_window_div .parent_line .catalog-filtr__check:checked');
			var cur_partner_value = '';
			if(cur_partner.length > 0) {
				cur_partner_value = cur_partner[0].value;
				params = params + '&parID=' + cur_partner_value.substring(6);
			}

			/*$('#main_block').hide();
			$('#close_line').hide();
			$('#waiting').show();*/
			if(href_str != '') {
				if(file_format == 'xml') {
					window.location.href = '/upload/catalog_files/'+href_str+'.xml';
				}
				else if(file_format == 'yml') {
					window.location.href = '/upload/catalog_files/yandex/'+href_str+'.xml';
				}
				else if(file_format == 'csv') {
					window.location.href = '/upload/catalog_files/'+href_str+'.csv';
				}
				else {
					window.location.href = '/upload/catalog_files/'+href_str+'.xls';
				}
			}
			else {
				window.location.href = 'specification_xls.php?FILE='+file_format+'&ACTION=FILTER' + params;
			}
		}

		function set_unset_filter_price(obj)
		{
			$(obj).parent().parent().find(".catalog-filtr__check").attr("checked", false);
			$(obj).prop("checked", true);
			if($('#a_pdf').length) {
				downloadPhotos();
			}

		}

			href_arr["NOVYY_TOVAR_ODEON_LIGHT_EXCLUSIVE_inter"] = 'https://disk.yandex.ru/d/6wHQuZFSrxIOcw';

			var filters 	= $('#modal_window_div .filter_line .catalog-filtr__check:checked');
			for(var i=0; i<filters.length; i++)
			{
				var str = '';
				child_data = filters[i];
				var value = child_data.value;
				if (child_data.value == 'ODEON LIGHT')
					{str = 'ODEON';}
				else if (child_data.value == 'NOVOTECH LAMP')
					{str = 'NOVOTECH_LAMP';}
				else if (child_data.value == 'ODEON LIGHT EXCLUSIVE')
					{str = 'ODEON_LIGHT_EXCLUSIVE';}
				else {
					str = child_data.value;
				}

				if($(child_data).attr('data-new-property') == 'PROPERTY_NOVYY_TOVAR' && str != '')
					{str = 'NOVYY_TOVAR_' + str;}

				var href_jpg = document.getElementById('a_jpg');
				var href_tiff = document.getElementById('a_tiff');
				var href_inter = document.getElementById('a_inter');
				var href_pdf = document.getElementById('a_pdf');
				href_jpg.style.display = 'none';
				href_tiff.style.display = 'none';
				href_inter.style.display = 'none';
				href_pdf.style.display = 'none';

				href_jpg.href = '';
				href_tiff.href = '';
				href_inter.href = '';
				href_pdf.href = '';

				if (!href_arr[str+'_jpg'] == '')
					{
						href_jpg.style.display = 'block';
						href_jpg.href = href_arr[str+'_jpg'];
					}
				if (!href_arr[str+'_tiff'] == '')
					{
						href_tiff.style.display = 'block';
						href_tiff.href = href_arr[str+'_tiff'];
					}
				if (!href_arr[str+'_pdf'] == '')
					{
						href_pdf.style.display = 'block';
						href_pdf.href = href_arr[str+'_pdf'];
					}
				if (!href_arr[str+'_inter'] == '')
					{
						href_inter.style.display = 'block';
						href_inter.href = href_arr[str+'_inter'];
					}
			}
		}

	window.onscroll = function()
	{
		console.log(document.body.scrollHeight);
		console.log(document.body.clientHeight);
		if (document.body.scrollHeight - (document.body.scrollTop  || window.pageYOffset) === document.body.clientHeight)
		{
			var obj_line = document.getElementById('more_line');
			var obj_count = document.getElementById('more_count');
			if(!(obj_line == null))
			{
				var line= obj_line.value;
				var cnt = obj_count.value;
				add_new_items(3,cnt, line);
			}
		}
		if (document.body.scrollTop || window.pageYOffset > 640) {
			$('#button_up').show();
		} else {
			$('#button_up').hide();
		}

	}

	function button_up_click()
	{
		window.scrollTo(0,0);
	}


	function bsk_click(id, quan)
	{
		var inp = document.getElementById(id);
		inp.value = Number(inp.value) + quan;
		if(isNaN(inp.value))
			inp.value = 1;

		if(Number(inp.value) <= 0)
			inp.value = 1;
	}

	function onMaterialClick() {
		$('#material_button').hide();
		$('#news').hide();
		$('#material').show();
	}

</script>
